# Security Audit: Missing Authentication Middleware in HTTP Handlers

## Your Task

Find Go source files in the Loki and Mimir repositories that register HTTP handlers or routes without applying authentication middleware such as `middleware.AuthenticateUser`.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

## Documentation

Instructions for documentation authoring in Markdown files.

DOCS.md contains all the Docs AI toolkit docs in one file.

## Role

Act as an experienced software engineer and technical writer for Grafana Labs.

Write for software developers and engineers who understand general programming concepts.

Focus on practical implementation and clear problem-solving guidance.

### Grafana

Use full product names on first mention, then short names:

- Grafana Alloy (full), Alloy (short)
- Grafana Beyla (full), Beyla (short)

Use "OpenTelemetry Collector" on first mention, then "Collector" for subsequent references.
Keep full name for distributions, headings, and links.

Always use "Grafana Cloud" in full.

Use complete terms:

- "OpenTelemetry" (not "OTel")
- "Kubernetes" (not "K8s")

Present observability signals in order: metrics, logs, traces, and profiles.

Focus content on Grafana solutions when discussing integrations or migrations.

## Style

### Structure

Structure articles into sections with headings.

Leave Markdown front matter content between two triple dashes `---`.

The front matter YAML `title` and the content h1 (#) heading should be the same.
Make sure there's an h1 heading in the content; this redundancy is required.

Always include copy after a heading or between headings, for example:

```markdown
## Heading

Immediately followed by copy and not another heading.

## Sub heading
```

The immediate copy after a heading should introduce and provide an overview of what's covered in the section.

Start articles with an introduction that covers the goal of the article. Example goals:

- Learn concepts
- Set up or install something
- Configure something
- Use a product to solve a busines
... (truncated)

   689→func (hs *HTTPServer) metricsEndpoint(ctx *web.Context) {
   690→	if !hs.Cfg.MetricsEndpointEnabled {
   691→		return
   692→	}
   693→
   694→	if ctx.Req.Method != http.MethodGet || ctx.Req.URL.Path != "/metrics" {
   695→		return
   696→	}
   697→
   698→	if hs.metricsEndpointBasicAuthEnabled() && !BasicAuthenticatedRequest(ctx.Req, hs.Cfg.MetricsEndpointBasicAuthUsername, hs.Cfg.MetricsEndpointBasicAuthPassword) {
   699→		ctx.Resp.Header().Set("WWW-Authenticate", `Basic realm="Grafana"`)
   700→		ctx.Resp.WriteHeader(http.StatusUnauthorized)
   701→		return
   702→	}
   703→
   704→	promhttp.
   705→		HandlerFor(hs.promGatherer, promhttp.HandlerOpts{EnableOpenMetrics: true}).
   706→		ServeHTTP(ctx.Resp, ctx.Req)
   707→}
   708→
   709→// healthzHandler always return 200 - Ok if Grafana's web server is running
   710→func (hs *HTTPServer) healthzHandler(ctx *web.Context) {
   711→	notHeadOrGet := ctx.Req.Method != http.MethodGet && ctx.Req.Method != http.MethodHead
   712→	if notHeadOrGet || ctx.Req.URL.Path != "/healthz" {
   713→		return
   714→	}
   715→
   716→	ctx.Resp.WriteHeader(http.StatusOK)
   717→	if _, err := ctx.Resp.Write([]byte("Ok")); err != nil {
   718→		hs.log.Error("could not write to response", "err", err)
   719→	}
   720→}

    19→func UploadErrorToStatusCode(err error) int {
    20→	switch {
    21→	case errors.Is(err, ErrStorageNotFound):
    22→		return 404
    23→
    24→	case errors.Is(err, ErrUnsupportedStorage):
    25→		return 400
    26→
    27→	case errors.Is(err, ErrValidationFailed):
    28→		return 400
    29→
    30→	case errors.Is(err, ErrQuotaReached):
    31→		return 400
    32→
    33→	case errors.Is(err, ErrFileAlreadyExists):
    34→		return 400
    35→
    36→	case errors.Is(err, ErrAccessDenied):
    37→		return 403
    38→
    39→	default:
    40→		return 500
    41→	}
    42→}

     1→package client
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"net/http"
     5→)
     6→
     7→const (
     8→	MimirTenantHeader        = "X-Scope-OrgID"
     9→	RemoteAlertmanagerHeader = "X-Remote-Alertmanager"
    10→)
    11→
    12→type MimirAuthRoundTripper struct {
    13→	TenantID string
    14→	Password string
    15→	Next     http.RoundTripper
    16→}
    17→
    18→// RoundTrip implements the http.RoundTripper interface
    19→// It adds an `X-Scope-OrgID` header with the TenantID if only provided with a tenantID or sets HTTP Basic Authentication if both
    20→// a tenantID and a password are provided.
    21→func (r *MimirAuthRoundTripper) RoundTrip(req *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {
    22→	req.Header.Set(RemoteAlertmanagerHeader, "true")
    23→	if r.TenantID != "" && r.Password == "" {
    24→		req.Header.Set(MimirTenantHeader, r.TenantID)
    25→	}
    26→
    27→	if r.TenantID != "" && r.Password != "" {
    28→		req.SetBasicAuth(r.TenantID, r.Password)
    29→	}
    30→
    31→	return r.Next.RoundTrip(req)
    32→}
    33→

    13→
    14→func (hs *HTTPServer) pluginMetricsEndpoint(ctx *web.Context) {
    15→	if !hs.Cfg.MetricsEndpointEnabled {
    16→		return
    17→	}
    18→
    19→	if ctx.Req.Method != http.MethodGet || !strings.HasPrefix(ctx.Req.URL.Path, "/metrics/plugins/") {
    20→		return
    21→	}
    22→
    23→	if hs.metricsEndpointBasicAuthEnabled() && !BasicAuthenticatedRequest(ctx.Req, hs.Cfg.MetricsEndpointBasicAuthUsername, hs.Cfg.MetricsEndpointBasicAuthPassword) {
    24→		ctx.Resp.WriteHeader(http.StatusUnauthorized)
    25→		return
    26→	}
    27→
    28→	pathParts := strings.SplitAfter(ctx.Req.URL.Path, "/")
    29→	pluginID := pathParts[len(pathParts)-1]
    30→
    31→	resp, err := hs.pluginClient.CollectMetrics(ctx.Req.Context(), &backend.CollectMetricsRequest{PluginContext: backend.PluginContext{PluginID: pluginID}})
    32→	if err != nil {
    33→		if errors.Is(err, plugins.ErrPluginNotRegistered) {
    34→			ctx.Resp.WriteHeader(http.StatusNotFound)
    35→			return
    36→		}
    37→
    38→		ctx.Resp.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)
    39→		return
    40→	}
    41→
    42→	ctx.Resp.Header().Set("Content-Type", "text/plain")
    43→	if _, err := ctx.Resp.Write(resp.PrometheusMetrics); err != nil {
    44→		hs.log.Error("Failed to write to response", "err", err)
    45→	}
    46→}

Based on my extensive research of the workspace:

**Key Finding:** The workspace contains `grafana/grafana` at commit `26d36ec` — this is Grafana's main dashboard/alerting repository, **not** separate Loki or Mimir repositories.

**What I searched for:**
- `middleware.AuthenticateUser` — **not present anywhere** in this codebase (this is a weaveworks/dskit pattern used in actual Loki/Mimir repos)
- HTTP route registrations without authentication middleware
- Loki/Mimir-compatible API handlers (found in `pkg/services/ngalert/api/`)

**What I found:**
- The ngalert package implements Loki/Mimir/Cortex-compatible APIs (`lotex_ruler.go`, `lotex_am.go`, generated API files)
- All these endpoints use `middleware.ReqSignedIn`, not `middleware.AuthenticateUser`
- Some Grafana routes are intentionally unauthenticated (login, snapshots, signup) but are unrelated to Loki/Mimir functionality

Since the actual Loki and Mimir repositories are not present in the workspace, no files matching the specific security pattern (`middleware.AuthenticateUser` missing from Loki/Mimir route registrations) could be identified. The answer file reflects this finding with an empty files/symbols list and a detailed text explanation.

This is appropriate for Grafana's session-based auth model, but differs from the multi-tenant `middleware.AuthenticateUser` pattern used in the actual Loki and Mimir codebases.\\n\\nNo Go source files in this repository register Loki- or Mimir-compatible HTTP handlers completely without authentication middleware.
